\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00015}00015\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}"{}"{}Preprocess\ images\ and\ bounding\ boxes\ for\ detection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00016}00016\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00017}00017\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{We\ perform\ two\ sets\ of\ operations\ in\ preprocessing\ stage:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00018}00018\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{(a)\ operations\ that\ are\ applied\ to\ both\ training\ and\ testing\ data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00019}00019\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{(b)\ operations\ that\ are\ applied\ only\ to\ training\ data\ for\ the\ purpose\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00020}00020\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ data\ augmentation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00021}00021\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00022}00022\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{A\ preprocessing\ function\ receives\ a\ set\ of\ inputs,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00023}00023\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{e.g.\ an\ image\ }\textcolor{keywordflow}{and}\ bounding\ boxes,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00024}00024\ performs\ an\ operation\ on\ them,\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{and}\ returns\ them.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00025}00025\ Some\ examples\ are:\ randomly\ cropping\ the\ image,\ randomly\ mirroring\ the\ image,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00026}00026\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ randomly\ changing\ the\ brightness,\ contrast,\ hue\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00027}00027\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ randomly\ jittering\ the\ bounding\ boxes.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00028}00028\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00029}00029\ The\ preprocess\ function\ receives\ a\ tensor\_dict\ which\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{is}\ a\ dictionary\ that\ maps}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00030}00030\ different\ field\ names\ to\ their\ tensors.\ For\ example,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00031}00031\ tensor\_dict[fields.InputDataFields.image]\ holds\ the\ image\ tensor.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00032}00032\ The\ image\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{is}\ a\ rank\ 4\ tensor:\ [1,\ height,\ width,\ channels]\ \textcolor{keyword}{with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00033}00033\ dtype=tf.float32.\ The\ groundtruth\_boxes\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{is}\ a\ rank\ 2\ tensor:\ [N,\ 4]\ where}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00034}00034\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{in}\ each\ row\ there\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{is}\ a\ box\ \textcolor{keyword}{with}\ [ymin\ xmin\ ymax\ xmax].}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00035}00035\ Boxes\ are\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{in}\ normalized\ coordinates\ meaning}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00036}00036\ their\ coordinate\ values\ range\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{in}\ [0,\ 1]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00037}00037\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00038}00038\ To\ preprocess\ multiple\ images\ \textcolor{keyword}{with}\ the\ same\ operations\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{in}\ cases\ where}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00039}00039\ nondeterministic\ operations\ are\ used,\ a\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classdetection__utils_1_1core_1_1preprocessor__cache_1_1_preprocessor_cache}{preprocessor\_cache.PreprocessorCache}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00040}00040\ object\ can\ be\ passed\ into\ the\ preprocess\ function\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{or}\ individual\ operations.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00041}00041\ All\ nondeterministic\ operations\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{except}\ random\_jitter\_boxes\ support\ caching.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00042}00042\ E.g.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00043}00043\ Let\ tensor\_dict\{1,2,3,4,5\}\ be\ copies\ of\ the\ same\ inputs.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00044}00044\ Let\ preprocess\_options\ contain\ nondeterministic\ operation(s)\ excluding}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00045}00045\ random\_jitter\_boxes.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00046}00046\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00047}00047\ cache1\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classdetection__utils_1_1core_1_1preprocessor__cache_1_1_preprocessor_cache}{preprocessor\_cache.PreprocessorCache}}()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00048}00048\ cache2\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classdetection__utils_1_1core_1_1preprocessor__cache_1_1_preprocessor_cache}{preprocessor\_cache.PreprocessorCache}}()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00049}00049\ a\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetection__utils_1_1core_1_1preprocessor_a7806fdbc8bcd478d285ebb8873c8321c}{preprocess}}(tensor\_dict1,\ preprocess\_options,\ preprocess\_vars\_cache=cache1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00050}00050\ b\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetection__utils_1_1core_1_1preprocessor_a7806fdbc8bcd478d285ebb8873c8321c}{preprocess}}(tensor\_dict2,\ preprocess\_options,\ preprocess\_vars\_cache=cache1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00051}00051\ c\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetection__utils_1_1core_1_1preprocessor_a7806fdbc8bcd478d285ebb8873c8321c}{preprocess}}(tensor\_dict3,\ preprocess\_options,\ preprocess\_vars\_cache=cache2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00052}00052\ d\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetection__utils_1_1core_1_1preprocessor_a7806fdbc8bcd478d285ebb8873c8321c}{preprocess}}(tensor\_dict4,\ preprocess\_options,\ preprocess\_vars\_cache=cache2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00053}00053\ e\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetection__utils_1_1core_1_1preprocessor_a7806fdbc8bcd478d285ebb8873c8321c}{preprocess}}(tensor\_dict5,\ preprocess\_options)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00054}00054\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00055}00055\ Then\ correspondings\ tensors\ of\ object\ pairs\ (a,b)\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{and}\ (c,d)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00056}00056\ are\ guaranteed\ to\ be\ equal\ element-\/wise,\ but\ the\ equality\ of\ any\ other\ object}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00057}00057\ pair\ cannot\ be\ determined.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00058}00058\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00059}00059\ Important\ Note:\ In\ tensor\_dict,\ images\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{is}\ a\ rank\ 4\ tensor,\ but\ preprocessing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00060}00060\ functions\ receive\ a\ rank\ 3\ tensor\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ processing\ the\ image.\ Thus,\ inside\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00061}00061\ preprocess\ function\ we\ squeeze\ the\ image\ to\ become\ a\ rank\ 3\ tensor\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{and}\ then}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00062}00062\ we\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{pass}\ it\ to\ the\ functions.\ At\ the\ end\ of\ the\ preprocess\ we\ expand\ the\ image}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{preprocessor_8py_source_l00063}00063\ back\ to\ rank\ 4.}
